 unhone man bana liya he ki is baar emsidi main phir BJP ko jitaayenge or kejariwal kaa patta saaf kar denge
 There is a severe shortage of cheap and affordable homes in the property world
 bilderon kaa jor mahange aaleeshaan makaan banane par rahaa he, jise lakjri segment bhi kaha jataa hai
 It would be ironic that real estate builders show little interest in the housing sector where homes are most needed
 baat ho rahi he 20 lakh se kam keemat ke makaanon kii, jo ki kifayati gharon kii shrenee main aate hai
 There is a shortage of about 20 million households in India and 95% of these households are economically weaker sections (EWS) and low income groups (LIG)
 builder kifayati ghar banane vaale nirmaan se isliye dur rahe hai, kyonki yahaan profit margin mahange gharon ke mukaable kam rahata he
 Increasing cost of land Due to increasing cost of construction, the construction of affordable houses does not seem to be a profitable deal for most builders
 modi sarkaar ke shahari vikaas or houseing agenda main sabake liye ghar kaa mudda praathamikta ke taur par shaamil kiya gaya he
 An ambitious target has been set to give each family a home by 2022
 is sambandh main kifayati makaanon ko banane vaale bilderon ko badhaava dene kii jarurat he
 The government can encourage builders to build houses in the affordable sector by providing necessary infrastructure such as electricity, water and a better environment for rapid investment in necessary clearances
 builder aashaa bhari nigahon se sarkaar kii ore dekh rahe hai
 Company director Raghav Garg, who came to participate in the Property India show to be aired on NDTV India, has said that the problems and difficulties faced in building small and affordable homes are not less than a big project, but the builder gets less profit from cheap homes
 Get
 jameen kii laagat se lekar manzooriyon main utana hi mehnat kerani padati he, jitna bade gharon ke liye
 The government needs to make this segment more attractive to builders
 to kya kifayati gharon ke nirmaan main kam munaafe kii takreer hi sabase badi aadchan he? jaani-maani real estate kansaltent diloit lo inakam houseing ke lead vikram jain ne property india main baatcheet main tasviir kaa doosraa pahalu saamne rakhaa
 He says that builders are making profits from low income housing and this is why 100 builders have taken up the task of constructing about 78000 houses in 23 cities
 agar yah munaafe kaa sauda na hota to ye mumkin nahin tha
 Mahindra Lifespaces, the real estate company of the Mahindra Group, has come forward to build affordable homes, which is going to start construction of affordable houses near Mumbai and Chennai, two big metros
 ye company 20 lakh se kam keemat kii laagat main mumbai ke paas boiser or chennai ke paas avadi main saste or chote gharon kaa nirmaan karegi
 The special thing is that the company sees the segment of affordable homes as a big business opportunity
 yah baat company kii pramukh anitha arjunadas ne media se kahi
 They believe that building cheap homes is not a social service and earning from low cost houses can also be done
 isse pehle tata samooh ne kai saal pehle mumbai ke paas boiser main saste gharon kii yojana shuru kii, jise khariddaaron ne jabardast tareeke haathon-haath liya
 According to them, this effort will be successful because they will implement it with a manufacturing mind set
 iskaa matlab he pre fabricated strekcharon ko nirmaan kshetra main jamaakar nirmaan ko gati dena, lekin ensiaar ke ghaziabad main saste ghar banane vaale bilderon main se ek garg samooh ke raghav garg ke mutabik, is tarah kii takneekee kii ijazat bade bilderon kii jeb hi detii he chote bilderon kii nahin
 While builders need to come forward to build cheaper homes, the government also needs to encourage the construction of affordable houses
 desh main shaharikaran jis raftaar se bad rahaa he us lihaaj se aane vaale samay main lakhon karodon log gramin ilaakon se behatar jindagi kii chahat main shaharon kaa rukh karenge
 According to the Planning Commission report, by 2031, the population in cities of the country would have been 60 crore, which would be 59 percent more than in 2011
 aise main kifayati ghar vakt kii maang he, jisase munafa kamanaa bhi mumkin he, agar builder baari munaafe ke margin kii ummid ko kam karen
 Experts believe that this can be an attractive business policy for the long term, where the profit will be determined by the number of units, not every unit
 dilli uniwarsity ke ramajas college main ek seminar ko lekar do chaatr sanghathanon ke bich hue vivaad ko lekar soshal media par abivipi ke virodh main aawaaj uthaakar charchaa main ai gurmeher cor ab ek blog ko lekar charchaa main hai
 After her post on social media went viral against ABVP, the student Gurmehar Kaur alleged that she received threats of rape
 iske baad raajnneeti se lekar cricketer jagat tak kai tarah kii tippaniyan saamne ai thim
